msg:This trip to Xishuangbanna was a very satisfying and comfortable journey. I feel that most of the comfort was provided by the hotel. Before going, I was struggling with the choice of modern experience, Dai style, and convenient location. Hotels that meet these points at the same time are so expensive ğŸ˜‚. Yuelianzhuang Lianfu just meets all the requirements.
First of all, the location. It is undoubtedly very convenient to go to the scenic spot in Gaozhuang. The surprise of this hotel is that it is located on the side of Gaozhuang, quiet in the hustle and bustle, perfectly avoiding the shortcomings of the noisy Gaozhuang. Then the hotel also has a battery car pick-up service, which is free at any time in the Gaozhuang scenic area. Every night we go out to eat and eat. It is super cool at night in this season, and the experience of riding an open-top battery car is overwhelming.
Secondly, the room, Dai style, strong Southeast Asian style, we booked a two-bedroom suite, the off-season price is okay, which is the price of a five-star hotel in a general scenic area, and the room also has a small couch that can be used as a sofa. And the room is relatively new, without the damage of the old hotel, and there is no odor of new decoration. In addition, the shampoo provided by the family is very useful. After washing, the hair is smooth and refreshing. They also gave me a children's shampoo and care set. My child is too young to use it, but it looks very good, so I took it away when I left.
Finally, the service must be mentioned. The service is amazing. Their family provides butler-style service. Contact the customer in advance, assign a butler, and then contact the butler for everything. The Xiaoyan butler we assigned is a Dai guy. He is very enthusiastic and thoughtful. The other front desk and restaurant service staff of the hotel are also very polite and responsible. The overall feeling is very gentle and kind. And! His family provides a super rich breakfast. The wontons are handmade and freshly wrapped. I strongly recommend it. The rice noodles taste great. The dishes include meat or prawns. There is also a delicate afternoon tea. The brown sugar jelly is super delicious, and the potato chips salad is also delicious. The hotel's swimming pool is very clean. I swam for two or three days. There is also a sauna room. My mother-in-law went to steam it three times. Because it is tiring to take care of children, we only go to one attraction every day. Most of the other time we spend in the hotel, eating, drinking and playing, and it is not boring at all.
To sum up, the whole family is very satisfied with this hotel. I plan to go to Xishuangbanna again when the children are older and stay at this hotel again.
